If the container is not running, container runtime can choose\n78:     // to either create a new log file and return nil, or return an error.\n79:     // Once it returns error, new container log file MUST NOT be created.\n80:     rpc ReopenContainerLog(ReopenContainerLogRequest) returns (ReopenContainerLogResponse) {}\n81: \n82:     // ExecSync runs a command in a container synchronously.\n83:     rpc ExecSync(ExecSyncRequest) returns (ExecSyncResponse) {}\n84:     // Exec prepares a streaming endpoint to execute a command in the container.\n85:     rpc Exec(ExecRequest) returns (ExecResponse) {}\n86:     // Attach prepares a streaming endpoint to attach to a running container.\n87:     rpc Attach(AttachRequest) returns (AttachResponse) {}\n88:     // PortForward prepares a streaming endpoint to forward ports from a PodSandbox.\n89:     rpc PortForward(PortForwardRequest) returns (PortForwardResponse) {}\n90: \n91:     // ContainerStats returns stats of the container. If the container does not\n92:     // exist, the call returns an error.\n93:     rpc ContainerStats(ContainerStatsRequest) returns (ContainerStatsResponse) {}\n94:     // ListContainerStats returns stats of all running containers.\n95:     rpc ListContainerStats(ListContainerStatsRequest) returns (ListContainerStatsResponse) {}\n96: \n97:     // PodSandboxStats returns stats of the pod sandbox. If the pod sandbox does not\n98:     // exist, the call returns an error.\n99:     rpc PodSandboxStats(PodSandboxStatsRequest) returns (PodSandboxStatsResponse) {}\n100:     // ListPodSandboxStats returns stats of the pod sandboxes matching a filter.\n101:     rpc ListPodSandboxStats(ListPodSandboxStatsRequest) returns (ListPodSandboxStatsResponse) {}\n102: \n103:     // UpdateRuntimeConfig updates the runtime configuration based on the given request.\n104:     rpc UpdateRuntimeConfig(UpdateRuntimeConfigRequest) returns (UpdateRuntimeConfigResponse) {}\n105: \n106:     // Status returns the status of the runtime.\n107:     rpc Status(StatusRequest) returns (StatusResponse) {}\n108: \n109:     // CheckpointContainer checkpoints a container\n110:     rpc CheckpointContainer(CheckpointContainerRequest) returns (CheckpointContainerResponse) {}\n111: \n112:     // GetContainerEvents gets container events from the CRI runtime\n113:     rpc GetContainerEvents(GetEventsRequest) returns (stream ContainerEventResponse) {}\n114: \n115:     // ListMetricDescriptors gets the descriptors for the metrics that will be returned in ListPodSandboxMetrics.\n116:     // This list should be static at startup: either the client and server restart together when\n117:     // adding or removing metrics descriptors, or they should not change.\n118:     // Put differently, if ListPodSandboxMetrics references a name that is not described in the initial\n119:     // ListMetricDescriptors call, then the metric will not be broadcasted.\n120:     rpc ListMetricDescriptors(ListMetricDescriptorsRequest) returns (ListMetricDescriptorsResponse) {}\n121: \n122:     // ListPodSandboxMetrics gets pod sandbox metrics from CRI Runtime\n123:     rpc ListPodSandboxMetrics(ListPodSandboxMetricsRequest) returns (ListPodSandboxMetricsResponse) {}\n124: \n125:     // RuntimeConfig returns configuration information of the runtime.\n126:     // A couple of notes:\n127:     // - The RuntimeConfigRequest object is not to be confused with the contents of UpdateRuntimeConfigRequest.\n128:     //   The former is for having runtime tell Kubelet what to do, the latter vice versa.\n129:     // - It is the expectation of the Kubelet that these fields are static for the lifecycle of the Kubelet.\n130:     //   The Kubelet will not re-request the RuntimeConfiguration after startup, and CRI implementations should\n131:     //   avoid updating them without a full node reboot.\n132:     rpc RuntimeConfig(RuntimeConfigRequest) returns (RuntimeConfigResponse) {}\n133: \n134:     // UpdatePodSandboxResources synchronously updates the PodSandboxConfig with\n135:     // the pod-level resource configuration. This method is called _after_ the\n136:     // Kubelet reconfigures the pod-level cgroups.\n137:     // This request is treated as best effort, and failure will not block the\n138:     // Kubelet with proceeding with a resize.\n139:     rpc UpdatePodSandboxResources(UpdatePodSandboxResourcesRequest) returns (UpdatePodSandboxResourcesResponse) {}\n140: }\n141: \n142: // ImageService defines the public APIs for managing images.\n143: service ImageService {\n144:     // ListImages lists existing images.\n145:     rpc ListImages(ListImagesRequest) returns (ListImagesResponse) {}\n146:     // ImageStatus returns the status of the image. If the image is not\n147:     // present, returns a response with ImageStatusResponse.Image set to\n148:     // nil.\n149:     rpc ImageStatus(ImageStatusRequest) returns (ImageStatusResponse) {}\n150:     // PullImage pulls an image with authentication config.\n151:     rpc PullImage(PullImageRequest) returns (PullImageResponse) {}\n152:     // RemoveImage removes the image.\n153:     // This call is idempotent, and must not return an error if the image has\n154:     // already been removed.\n155:     // Note that if the image is referenced by multiple tags (even across different repositories\n156:     // if they resolve to the same image digest), removing the image by a single tag\n157:     // will remove all of its tags. For example, if `repo/image:v1` and `another_repo/image:latest`\n158:     // point to the same image, removing `repo/image:v1` will also remove `another_repo/image:latest`.\n159:     // The next call to ListImages, ImageStatus, ImageFsInfo will not return this image.\n160:     // The resources (e.g. disk space) may be cleaned asynchronously\n161:     // and not guaranteed to be cleaned up by the time this method returns.\n162:     rpc RemoveImage(RemoveImageRequest) returns (RemoveImageResponse) {}\n163:     // ImageFSInfo returns information of the filesystem that is used to store images.\n164:     // Usage information may include images that were removed, but are still being cleaned up.\n165:     rpc ImageFsInfo(ImageFsInfoRequest) returns (ImageFsInfoResponse) {}\n166: }\n167: \n168: message VersionRequest {\n169:     // Version of the kubelet runtime API.\n170:     string version = 1;\n171: }\n172: \n173: message VersionResponse {\n174:     // Version of the kubelet runtime API.\n175:     string version = 1;\n176:     // Name of the container runtime.\n177:     string runtime_name = 2;\n178:     // Version of the container runtime. The string must be\n179:     // semver-compatible.\n180:     string runtime_version = 3;\n181:     // API version of the container runtime. The string must be\n182:     // semver-compatible.\n183:     string runtime_api_version = 4;\n184: }\n185: \n186: // DNSConfig specifies the DNS servers and search domains of a sandbox.\n187: message DNSConfig {\n188:     // List of DNS servers of the cluster.\n189:     repeated string servers = 1;\n190:     // List of DNS search domains of the cluster.\n191:     repeated string searches = 2;\n192:     // List of DNS options. See https://linux.die.net/man/5/resolv.conf\n193:     // for all available options.\n194:     repeated string options = 3;\n195: }\n196: \n197: enum Protocol {\n198:     TCP = 0;\n199:     UDP = 1;\n200:     SCTP = 2;\n201: }\n202: \n203: // PortMapping specifies the port mapping configurations of a sandbox.\n204: message PortMapping {\n205:     // Protocol of the port mapping.\n206:     Protocol protocol = 1;\n207:     // Port number within the container. Default: 0 (not specified).\n208:     int32 container_port = 2;\n209:     // Port number on the host to map the container port to.\n210:     //\n211:     // * Valid host port range is 1-65535.\n212:     // * The value 0 has explicit semantic meaning: it indicates NO host port should be allocated.\n213:     // * The value 0 does NOT indicate dynamic port allocation. Future implementations\n214:     //   of dynamic allocation will use different values/semantics.\n215:     // * Implementations MUST handle the case where this field is explicitly set to 0,\n216:     //   This field SHOULD be omitted when no port is required.\n217:     //\n218:     // Default: If omitted, container port will not be exposed on the host.\n219:     int32 host_port = 3;\n220:     // Host IP.\n221:     string host_ip = 4;\n222: }\n223: \n224: enum MountPropagation {\n225:     // No mount propagation (\"rprivate\" in Linux terminology).\n226:     PROPAGATION_PRIVATE = 0;\n227:     // Mounts get propagated from the host to the container (\"rslave\" in Linux).\n228:     PROPAGATION_HOST_TO_CONTAINER = 1;\n229:     // Mounts get propagated from the host to the container and from the\n230:     // container to the host (\"rshared\" in Linux).\n231:     PROPAGATION_BIDIRECTIONAL = 2;\n232: }\n233: \n234: // Mount specifies a host volume to mount into a container.\n235: message Mount {\n236:     // Path of the mount within the container.\n237:     string container_path = 1;\n238:     // Path of the mount on the host. Has to be empty if the image field below\n239:     // is provided, because those fields are mutually exclusive. If the image\n240:     // field below is nil and the host path doesn't exist, then runtimes should\n241:     // report an error. If the hostpath is a symbolic link, runtimes should\n242:     // follow the symlink and mount the real destination to container.\n243:     string host_path = 2;\n244:     // If set, the mount is read-only.\n245:     bool readonly = 3;\n246:     // If set, the mount needs SELinux relabeling.\n247:     bool selinux_relabel = 4;\n248:     // Requested propagation mode.\n249:     MountPropagation propagation = 5;\n250:     // UidMappings specifies the runtime UID mappings for the mount.\n251:     repeated IDMapping uidMappings = 6;\n252:     // GidMappings specifies the runtime GID mappings for the mount.\n253:     repeated IDMapping gidMappings = 7;\n254:     // If set to true, the mount is made recursive read-only.\n255:     // In this CRI API, recursive_read_only is a plain true/false boolean, although its equivalent\n256:     // in the Kubernetes core API is a quaternary that can be nil, \"Enabled\", \"IfPossible\", or \"Disabled\".\n257:     // kubelet translates that quaternary value in the core API into a boolean in this CRI API.\n258:     // Remarks:\n259:     // - nil is just treated as false\n260:     // - when set to true, readonly must be explicitly set to true, and propagation must be PRIVATE (0).\n261:     // - (readonly == false && recursive_read_only == false) does not make the mount read-only.\n262:     bool recursive_read_only = 8;\n263:     // Mount an image reference (image ID, with or without digest), which is a\n264:     // special use case for image volume mounts. If this field is set, then\n265:     // host_path should be unset. All image mounts are per feature definition\n266:     // readonly (noexec). The kubelet does an PullImage RPC and evaluates the returned\n267:     // PullImageResponse.image_ref value, which is then set to the\n268:     // ImageSpec.image field. Runtimes are expected to mount the image as\n269:     // required.\n270:     // Introduced in the Image Volume Source KEP: https://kep.k8s.io/4639\n271:     ImageSpec image = 9;\n272:     // Specific image sub path to be used from inside the image instead of its\n273:     // root, only necessary if the above image field is set. If the sub path is\n274:     // not empty and does not exist in the image, then runtimes should fail and\n275:     // return an error.\n276:     // Introduced in the Image Volume Source KEP beta graduation: https://kep.k8s.io/4639\n277:     string image_sub_path = 10;\n278: }\n279: \n280: // IDMapping describes host to container ID mappings for a pod sandbox.\n281: message IDMapping {\n282:     // HostId is the id on the host.\n283:     uint32 host_id = 1;\n284:     // ContainerId is the id in the container.\n285:     uint32 container_id = 2;\n286:     // Length is the size of the range to map.\n287:     uint32 length = 3;\n288: }\n289: \n290: // A NamespaceMode describes the intended namespace configuration for each\n291: // of the namespaces (Network, PID, IPC) in NamespaceOption. Runtimes should\n292: // map these modes as appropriate for the technology underlying the runtime.\n293: enum NamespaceMode {\n294:     // A POD namespace is common to all containers in a pod.\n295:     // For example, a container with a PID namespace of POD expects to view\n296:     // all of the processes in all of the containers in the pod.\n297:     POD       = 0;\n298:     // A CONTAINER namespace is restricted to a single container.\n299:     // For example, a container with a PID namespace of CONTAINER expects to\n300:     // view only the processes in that container.\n301:     CONTAINER = 1;\n302:     // A NODE namespace is the namespace of the Kubernetes node.\n303:     // For example, a container with a PID namespace of NODE expects to view\n304:     // all of the processes on the host running the kubelet.\n305:     NODE      = 2;\n306:     // TARGET targets the namespace of another container. When this is specified,\n307:     // a target_id must be specified in NamespaceOption and refer to a container\n308:     // previously created with NamespaceMode CONTAINER. This containers namespace\n309:     // will be made to match that of container target_id.\n310:     // For example, a container with a PID namespace of TARGET expects to view\n311:     // all of the processes that container target_id can view.\n312:     TARGET    = 3;\n313: }\n314: \n315: // UserNamespace describes the intended user namespace configuration for a pod sandbox.\n316: message UserNamespace {\n317:     // Mode is the NamespaceMode for this UserNamespace.\n318:     // Note: NamespaceMode for UserNamespace currently supports only POD and NODE, not CONTAINER OR TARGET.\n319:     NamespaceMode mode = 1;\n320: \n321:     // Uids specifies the UID mappings for the user namespace.\n322:     repeated IDMapping uids = 2;\n323: \n324:     // Gids specifies the GID mappings for the user namespace.\n325:     repeated IDMapping gids = 3;\n326: }\n327: \n328: // NamespaceOption provides options for Linux namespaces.\n329: message NamespaceOption {\n330:     // Network namespace for this container/sandbox.\n331:     // Note: There is currently no way to set CONTAINER scoped network in the Kubernetes API.\n332:     // Namespaces currently set by the kubelet: POD, NODE\n333:     NamespaceMode network = 1;\n334:     // PID namespace for this container/sandbox.\n335:     // Note: The CRI default is POD, but the v1.PodSpec default is CONTAINER.\n336:     // The kubelet's runtime manager will set this to CONTAINER explicitly for v1 pods.\n337:     // Namespaces currently set by the kubelet: POD, CONTAINER, NODE, TARGET\n338:     NamespaceMode pid = 2;\n339:     // IPC namespace for this container/sandbox.\n340:     // Note: There is currently no way to set CONTAINER scoped IPC in the Kubernetes API.\n341:     // Namespaces currently set by the kubelet: POD, NODE\n342:     NamespaceMode ipc = 3;\n343:     // Target Container ID for NamespaceMode of TARGET. This container must have been\n344:     // previously created in the same pod. It is not possible to specify different targets\n345:     // for each namespace.\n346:     string target_id = 4;\n347:     // UsernsOptions for this pod sandbox.\n348:     // The Kubelet picks the user namespace configuration to use for the pod sandbox.  The mappings\n349:     // are specified as part of the UserNamespace struct.  If the struct is nil, then the POD mode\n350:     // must be assumed.  This is done for backward compatibility with older Kubelet versions that\n351:     // do not set a user namespace.\n352:     UserNamespace userns_options = 5;\n353: }\n354: \n355: // SupplementalGroupsPolicy defines how supplemental groups \n356: // of the first container processes are calculated.\n357: enum SupplementalGroupsPolicy {\n358:     // Merge means that the container's provided SupplementalGroups \n359:     // and FsGroup (specified in SecurityContext) will be merged with \n360:     // the primary user's groups as defined in the container image\n361:     // (in /etc/group).\n362:     Merge = 0;\n363:     // Strict means that the container's provided SupplementalGroups\n364:     // and FsGroup (specified in SecurityContext) will be used instead of \n365:     // any groups defined in the container image.\n366:     Strict = 1;\n367: }\n368: \n369: // Int64Value is the wrapper of int64.\n370: message Int64Value {\n371:     // The value.\n372:     int64 value = 1;\n373: }\n374: \n375: // LinuxSandboxSecurityContext holds linux security configuration that will be\n376: // applied to a sandbox. If a privileged container is to be executed within it, this\n403:     // MUST be true.\n404:     // This allows a sandbox to take additional security precautions if no\n405:     // privileged containers are expected to be run.\n406:     bool privileged = 6;\n407:     // Seccomp profile for the sandbox.\n408:     SecurityProfile seccomp = 9;\n409:     // AppArmor profile for the sandbox.\n410:     SecurityProfile apparmor = 10;\n411:     // Seccomp profile for the sandbox, candidate values are:\n412:     // * runtime/default: the default profile for the container runtime\n413:     // * unconfined: unconfined profile, ie, no seccomp sandboxing\n414:     // * localhost/<full-path-to-profile>: the profile installed on the node.\n415:     //   <full-path-to-profile> is the full path of the profile.\n416:     // Default: \"\", which is identical with unconfined.\n417:     string seccomp_profile_path = 7 [deprecated=true];\n418: }\n419: \n420: // A security profile which can be used for sandboxes and containers.\n421: message SecurityProfile {\n422:     // Available profile types.\n423:     enum ProfileType {\n424:         // The // A pre-defined profile on the node should be used.\n429:         Localhost = 2;\n430:     }\n431:     // Indicator which `ProfileType` should be applied.\n432:     ProfileType profile_type = However, the LogDirectory may contain\n487:     // binary log files with structured logging data from the individual\n488:     // containers. For example, the files might be newline separated JSON\n489:     // structured logs, systemd-journald journal files, gRPC trace files, etc.\n490:     // E.g.,\n491:     //     PodSandboxConfig.LogDirectory = `/var/log/pods/<NAMESPACE>_<NAME>_<UID>/`\n492:     //     ContainerConfig.LogPath = `containerName/Instance#.log`\n493:     string log_directory = 3;\n494:     // DNS config for the sandbox.\n495:     DNSConfig dns_config = 4;\n496:     // Port mappings for the sandbox.\n497:     repeated PortMapping port_mappings = 5;\n498:     // Key-value pairs that may be used to scope and select individual resources.\n499:     map<string, string> labels = 6;\n500:     // Unstructured key-value map that may be set by the kubelet to store and\n501:     // retrieve arbitrary metadata. string type = 3;\n899:     string level = 4;\n900: }\n901: \n902: // Capability contains the container capabilities to add or drop\n903: // Dropping a capability will drop it from all sets.\n904: // applied to a container.\n920: message LinuxContainerSecurityContext {\n921:     // Capabilities to add or drop.\n922:     Capability capabilities = 1;\n923:     // If set, run container in privileged mode.\n924:     // Privileged mode is incompatible with the following options. If any required condition is unmet, the node will be not ready.\n1687: // The required conditions include:\n1688: //   * RuntimeReady: RuntimeReady means the runtime is up and ready to accept\n1689: //   basic containers e.g. container only needs host network.\n1690: //   * NetworkReady: NetworkReady means the runtime network is up and ready to\n1691: //   accept containers which require container network.\n1692: // 2. ListContainerStats(context.Context, *ListContainerStatsRequest) (*ListContainerStatsResponse, error)\n    PodSandboxStats(context.Context, *PodSandboxStatsRequest) (*PodSandboxStats, error)\n    ListPodSandboxStats(context.Context, *ListPodSandboxStatsRequest) (*ListPodSandboxStatsResponse, error)\n    UpdateRuntimeConfig(context.Context, *UpdateRuntimeConfigRequest) (*UpdateRuntimeConfigResponse, error)\n    Status(context.Context, *StatusRequest) (*StatusResponse, error)\n    CheckpointContainer(context.Context, *CheckpointContainerRequest) (*CheckpointContainerResponse, error)\n    GetContainerEvents(*GetEventsRequest, grpc.ServerStreamingServer[ContainerEventResponse]) error\n    ListMetricDescriptors(context.Context, *ListMetricDescriptorsRequest) (*ListMetricDescriptorsResponse, error)\n    ListPodSandboxMetrics(context.Context, *ListPodSandboxMetricsRequest) (*ListPodSandboxMetricsResponse, error)\n    RuntimeConfig(context.Context, *RuntimeConfigRequest) (*RuntimeConfigResponse, error)\n    UpdatePodSandboxResources(context.Context, *UpdatePodSandboxResourcesRequest) (*UpdatePodSandboxResourcesResponse, error)\n    mustEmbedUnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer()\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Part 2: Kubernetes Go API Interfaces\n\n### Location\n- **Path:** `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/services.go`\n\n### Purpose\nWhile the gRPC interface defines the wire protocol, Kubernetes also defines higher-level Go interfaces for internal use. These interfaces break down the functionality into smaller, more manageable chunks:\n\n### Main Interfaces\n\n1. **RuntimeVersioner**\n   - `Version(ctx context.Context, apiVersion string) (*runtimeapi.VersionResponse, error)`\n\n2. **PodSandboxManager**\n   - `RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, config *runtimeapi.PodSandboxConfig, runtimeHandler string) (string, error)`\n   - `StopPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, podSandboxID string) error`\n   - `RemovePodSandbox(ctx context.Context, podSandboxID string) error`\n   - `PodSandboxStatus(ctx context.Context, podSandboxID string, verbose bool) (*runtimeapi.PodSandboxStatusResponse, error)`\n   - `ListPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, filter *runtimeapi.PodSandboxFilter) ([]*runtimeapi.PodSandbox, error)`\n   - `PortForward(ctx context.Context, request *runtimeapi.PortForwardRequest) (*runtimeapi.PortForwardResponse, error)`\n   - `UpdatePodSandboxResources(ctx context.Context, request *runtimeapi.UpdatePodSandboxResourcesRequest) (*runtimeapi.UpdatePodSandboxResourcesResponse, error)`\n\n3. **ContainerManager**\n   - `CreateContainer(ctx context.Context, podSandboxID string, config *runtimeapi.ContainerConfig, sandboxConfig *runtimeapi.PodSandboxConfig) (string, error)`\n   - `StartContainer(ctx context.Context, containerID string) error`\n   - `StopContainer(ctx context.Context, containerID string, timeout int64) error`\n   - `RemoveContainer(ctx context.Context, containerID string) error`\n   - `ListContainers(ctx context.Context, filter *runtimeapi.ContainerFilter) ([]*runtimeapi.Container, error)`\n   - `ContainerStatus(ctx context.Context, containerID string, verbose bool) (*runtimeapi.ContainerStatusResponse, error)`\n   - `UpdateContainerResources(ctx context.Context, containerID string, resources *runtimeapi.ContainerResources) error`\n   - `ExecSync(ctx context.Context, containerID string, cmd []string, timeout time.Duration) (stdout []byte, stderr []byte, err error)`\n   - `Exec(ctx context.Context, request *runtimeapi.ExecRequest) (*runtimeapi.ExecResponse, error)`\n   - `Attach(ctx context.Context, req *runtimeapi.AttachRequest) (*runtimeapi.AttachResponse, error)`\n   - `ReopenContainerLog(ctx context.Context, ContainerID string) error`\n   - `CheckpointContainer(ctx context.Context, options *runtimeapi.CheckpointContainerRequest) error`\n   - `GetContainerEvents(ctx context.Context, containerEventsCh chan *runtimeapi.ContainerEventResponse, connectionEstablishedCallback func(runtimeapi.RuntimeService_GetContainerEventsClient)) error`\n\n4. **ContainerStatsManager**\n   - `ContainerStats(ctx context.Context, containerID string) (*runtimeapi.ContainerStats, error)`\n   - `ListContainerStats(ctx context.Context, filter *runtimeapi.ContainerStatsFilter) ([]*runtimeapi.ContainerStats, error)`\n   - `PodSandboxStats(ctx context.Context, podSandboxID string) (*runtimeapi.PodSandboxStats, error)`\n   - `ListPodSandboxStats(ctx context.Context, filter *runtimeapi.PodSandboxStatsFilter) ([]*runtimeapi.PodSandboxStats, error)`\n   - `ListMetricDescriptors(ctx context.Context) ([]*runtimeapi.MetricDescriptor, error)`\n   - `ListPodSandboxMetrics(ctx context.Context) ([]*runtimeapi.PodSandboxMetrics, error)`\n\n5. **RuntimeService** (Composite Interface)\n   - Combines: RuntimeVersioner, ContainerManager, PodSandboxManager, ContainerStatsManager\n   - Additional methods:\n     - `UpdateRuntimeConfig(ctx context.Context, runtimeConfig *runtimeapi.RuntimeConfig) error`\n     - `Status(ctx context.Context, verbose bool) (*runtimeapi.StatusResponse, error)`\n     - `RuntimeConfig(ctx context.Context) (*runtimeapi.RuntimeConfigResponse, error)`\n     - `Close() error`\n\n6. **ImageManagerService**\n   - `ListImages(ctx context.Context, filter *runtimeapi.ImageFilter) ([]*runtimeapi.Image, error)`\n   - `ImageStatus(ctx context.Context, image *runtimeapi.ImageSpec, verbose bool) (*runtimeapi.ImageStatusResponse, error)`\n   - `PullImage(ctx context.Context, image *runtimeapi.ImageSpec, auth *runtimeapi.AuthConfig, podSandboxConfig *runtimeapi.PodSandboxConfig) (string, error)`\n   - `RemoveImage(ctx context.Context, image *runtimeapi.ImageSpec) error`\n   - `ImageFsInfo(ctx context.Context) (*runtimeapi.ImageFsInfoResponse, error)`\n   - `Close() error`\n\n---\n\n## Part 3: containerd's CRI Implementation\n\n### Location\n- **Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/containerd--317286ac`\n- **Main Paths:**\n  - `plugins/cri/` - Plugin registration and setup\n  - `internal/cri/server/` - Core CRI service implementation\n  - `internal/cri/instrument/` - Instrumentation and metrics\n  - `vendor/k8s.io/cri-api/` - Vendored Kubernetes CRI API types\n\n### Architecture Overview\n\ncontainerd implements the CRI interface through a multi-layered architecture:\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ gRPC Server (grpc.Server)                               │\n│ ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │\n│ │ criGRPCServer (runtime.RuntimeServiceServer impl)   │ │\n│ └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │\n└─────────────────────┬───────────────────────────────────┘\n                      │\n        ┌─────────────▼──────────────┐\n        │  instrument.NewService()   │\n        │ (instrumented wrapper)     │\n        └─────────────┬──────────────┘\n                      │\n        ┌─────────────▼──────────────────┐\n        │ criService struct              │\n        │ (main implementation)          │\n        └─────────────┬──────────────────┘\n                      │\n    ┌─────────────────┼─────────────────┐\n    │                 │                 │\n    ▼                 ▼                 ▼\nSandbox Ops      Container Ops    Image/Stats Ops\n```\n\n### 3.1 Plugin Registration & Initialization\n\n**File:** `plugins/cri/cri.go`\n\n```go\n// Registration entry point\nfunc init() {\n    defaultConfig := criconfig.DefaultServerConfig()\n    registry.Register(&plugin.Registration{\n        Type: plugins.GRPCPlugin,\n        ID:   \"cri\",\n        Requires: []plugin.Type{\n            plugins.CRIServicePlugin,       // Runtime service\n            plugins.PodSandboxPlugin,       // Pod sandbox support\n            plugins.SandboxControllerPlugin, // Sandbox controllers\n            plugins.NRIApiPlugin,           // Node Resource Interface\n            plugins.EventPlugin,            // Event handling\n            plugins.ServicePlugin,          // Services\n            plugins.LeasePlugin,            // Lease management\n            plugins.SandboxStorePlugin,     // Sandbox storage\n            plugins.TransferPlugin,         // Content transfer\n            plugins.WarningPlugin,          // Warning service\n        },\n        ConfigMigration: configMigration,\n        InitFn:          initCRIService,\n    })\n}\n\n// Initialization function\nfunc initCRIService(ic *plugin.InitContext) (interface{}, error) {\n    // 1. Load runtime service plugin\n    criRuntimePlugin, err := ic.GetByID(plugins.CRIServicePlugin, \"runtime\")\n\n    // 2. Load image service plugin\n    criImagePlugin, err := ic.GetByID(plugins.CRIServicePlugin, \"images\")\n\n    // 3. Create containerd client\n    client, err := containerd.New(\"\",\n        containerd.WithDefaultNamespace(constants.K8sContainerdNamespace),\n        containerd.WithDefaultPlatform(platforms.Default()),\n        containerd.WithInMemoryServices(ic),\n    )\n\n    // 4. Get sandbox controllers\n    sbControllers, err := getSandboxControllers(ic)\n\n    // 5. Create CRI service\n    s, rs, err := server.NewCRIService(&server.CRIServiceOptions{\n        RuntimeService:     criRuntimePlugin.(server.RuntimeService),\n        ImageService:       criImagePlugin.(server.ImageService),\n        StreamingConfig:    streamingConfig,\n        NRI:                getNRIAPI(ic),\n        Client:             client,\n        SandboxControllers: sbControllers,\n    })\n\n    // 6. Wrap in gRPC server\n    service := &criGRPCServer{\n        RuntimeServiceServer: rs,\n        ImageServiceServer:   is,\n        Closer:               s,\n        initializer:          s,\n    }\n\n    return service, nil\n}\n```\n\n### 3.2 Core CRI Service Implementation\n\n**File:** `internal/cri/server/service.go`\n\nThe `criService` struct implements the core logic:\n\n```go\ntype criService struct {\n    // Embedded unimplemented server to satisfy gRPC requirements\n    runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer\n    runtime.UnimplementedImageServiceServer\n\n    // Service dependencies\n    RuntimeService\n    ImageService\n\n    // Configuration\n    config criconfig.Config\n    imageFSPaths map[string]string\n    os osinterface.OS\n\n    // Storage and indexing\n    sandboxStore *sandboxstore.Store\n    sandboxNameIndex *registrar.Registrar  // Ensures unique sandbox names\n    containerStore *containerstore.Store\n    containerNameIndex *registrar.Registrar // Ensures unique container names\n\n    // Network management\n    netPlugin map[string]cni.CNI\n\n    // containerd client\n    client *containerd.Client\n\n    // Streaming support\n    streamServer streaming.Server\n\n    // Event monitoring\n    eventMonitor *events.EventMonitor\n\n    // Initialization flag\n    initialized atomic.Bool\n\n    // Network config monitoring\n    cniNetConfMonitor map[string]*cniNetConfSyncer\n\n    // Capabilities\n    allCaps []string\n\n    // Container events queue\n    containerEventsQ eventq.EventQueue[*runtime.ContainerEventResponse]\n\n    // Node Resource Interface\n    nri *nri.API\n\n    // Sandbox service\n    sandboxService sandboxService\n\n    // Runtime handlers and features\n    runtimeHandlers map[string]*runtime.RuntimeHandler\n    runtimeFeatures *runtime.RuntimeFeatures\n\n    // Stats collection\n    statsCollector *StatsCollector\n}\n```\n\n**Constructor:** `NewCRIService(options *CRIServiceOptions)`\n\nCreates a fully initialized CRI service with:\n- Sandbox and container stores\n- CNI network plugin initialization\n- Streaming server setup\n- Event monitoring\n- Stats collection\n\n### 3.3 RPC Method Implementation Examples\n\n#### RunPodSandbox Implementation\n\n**File:** `internal/cri/server/sandbox_run.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest)\n    (*runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    config := r.GetConfig()\n\n    // 1. Generate unique ID and name\n    id := util.GenerateID()\n    metadata := config.GetMetadata()\n    name := makeSandboxName(metadata)\n\n    // 2. Reserve the name (prevents concurrent creation with same name)\n    if err := c.sandboxNameIndex.Reserve(name, id); err != nil {\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to reserve sandbox name %q: %w\", name, err)\n    }\n    defer cleanup()\n\n    // 3. Create lease for sandbox lifecycle\n    leaseSvc := c.client.LeasesService()\n    ls, lerr := leaseSvc.Create(ctx, leases.WithID(id))\n\n    // 4. Setup network (CNI)\n    // - Call network plugin to setup network namespace\n    // - Allocate IP addresses for the pod\n\n    // 5. Create sandbox container (OCI spec from config)\n    // - Convert CRI PodSandboxConfig to OCI spec\n    // - Create containerd container\n\n    // 6. Start sandbox task\n    // - Start the sandbox task in containerd\n    // - Ensure sandbox is in ready state\n\n    // 7. Register sandbox in store\n    sandboxStore.Add(id, &Sandbox{\n        ID:     id,\n        Config: config,\n        State:  SANDBOX_READY,\n    })\n\n    // 8. Return response\n    return &runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse{\n        PodSandboxId: id,\n    }, nil\n}\n```\n\n**Key Details:**\n- Generates unique sandbox ID using `util.GenerateID()`\n- Reserves sandbox name to prevent concurrent duplicates\n- Creates lease for resource tracking\n- Sets up network using CNI plugins\n- Creates and starts sandbox task in containerd\n- Stores sandbox metadata in sandboxStore\n- Returns sandbox ID to caller (kubelet)\n\n#### StopPodSandbox Implementation\n\n**File:** `internal/cri/server/sandbox_stop.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) StopPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.StopPodSandboxRequest)\n    (*runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    podSandboxID := r.PodSandboxId\n    gracePeriod := r.Timeout\n\n    // 1. Lookup sandbox in store\n    sandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(podSandboxID)\n\n    // 2. Stop all containers in sandbox (forced termination)\n    for _, container := range c.containerStore.ListByPodID(podSandboxID) {\n        c.StopContainer(ctx, container.ID, gracePeriod)\n    }\n\n    // 3. Stop sandbox task in containerd\n    // - Send SIGTERM to sandbox\n    // - Wait for grace period\n    // - Force kill if still running\n\n    // 4. Teardown network (CNI)\n    // - Release IP addresses\n    // - Cleanup network namespace\n\n    // 5. Update sandbox state\n    sandbox.State = SANDBOX_NOTREADY\n    c.sandboxStore.Update(podSandboxID, sandbox)\n\n    // 6. Idempotent: return nil even if already stopped\n    return &runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n**Key Details:**\n- Idempotent operation (safe to call multiple times)\n- Forcibly terminates all containers in sandbox\n- Gracefully stops sandbox with timeout\n- Tears down network resources (CNI cleanup)\n- Updates sandbox state without removing from store\n\n#### RemovePodSandbox Implementation\n\n**File:** `internal/cri/server/sandbox_remove.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RemovePodSandbox(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.RemovePodSandboxRequest)\n    (*runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    podSandboxID := r.PodSandboxId\n\n    // 1. Lookup sandbox\n    sandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(podSandboxID)\n\n    // 2. Must be stopped first\n    if sandbox.State != SANDBOX_NOTREADY {\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"sandbox %q is still running\", podSandboxID)\n    }\n\n    // 3. Delete all containers in sandbox\n    for _, container := range c.containerStore.ListByPodID(podSandboxID) {\n        c.RemoveContainer(ctx, container.ID)\n    }\n\n    // 4. Delete sandbox container from containerd\n    // - Delete container task\n    // - Delete container\n    // - Delete snapshots\n\n    // 5. Release lease\n    leaseSvc := c.client.LeasesService()\n    leaseSvc.Delete(ctx, leases.WithID(podSandboxID))\n\n    // 6. Release sandbox name\n    c.sandboxNameIndex.ReleaseByName(sandbox.Name)\n\n    // 7. Remove from store\n    c.sandboxStore.Delete(podSandboxID)\n\n    // 8. Idempotent: return nil even if already removed\n    return &runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n**Key Details:**\n- Deletes all containers before removing sandbox\n- Removes containerd resources (snapshots, leases)\n- Releases reserved sandbox name\n- Idempotent (safe to call on already-removed sandbox)\n\n#### CreateContainer Implementation\n\n**File:** `internal/cri/server/container_create.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) CreateContainer(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.CreateContainerRequest)\n    (*runtime.CreateContainerResponse, error) {\n\n    podSandboxID := r.PodSandboxId\n    config := r.Config\n    sandboxConfig := r.SandboxConfig\n\n    // 1. Lookup parent sandbox\n    sandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(podSandboxID)\n\n    // 2. Generate container ID and name\n    containerID := util.GenerateID()\n    containerName := makeContainerName(metadata, sandbox.Config)\n\n    // 3. Reserve container name\n    if err := c.containerNameIndex.Reserve(containerName, containerID); err != nil {\n        return nil, err\n    }\n\n    // 4. Build OCI spec from CRI ContainerConfig\n    // - Start with runtime's base spec\n    // - Apply image config\n    // - Apply container config (env, mounts, resources, etc.)\n    // - Setup hostname, DNS, security context\n\n    // 5. Create container image snapshot\n    // - Pull image if needed\n    // - Create diff snapshot for container layers\n\n    // 6. Create containerd container\n    container, err := c.client.Containers().Create(ctx, &containers.Container{\n        ID:     containerID,\n        Image:  config.Image.Image,\n        Spec:   &ociSpec,\n        Snapshotter: snapshotterName,\n    })\n\n    // 7. Store container metadata\n    c.containerStore.Add(containerID, &Container{\n        ID:            containerID,\n        PodSandboxID:  podSandboxID,\n        Config:        config,\n        SandboxConfig: sandboxConfig,\n        ImageRef:      imageID,\n        State:         CONTAINER_CREATED,\n    })\n\n    // 8. Return container ID\n    return &runtime.CreateContainerResponse{\n        ContainerId: containerID,\n    }, nil\n}\n```\n\n**Key Details:**\n- Container created but NOT started yet\n- Generates OCI spec from CRI config\n- Pulls image if not available\n- Creates snapshots for container layers\n- Stores metadata for later retrieval\n- Actual task execution happens in StartContainer\n\n#### StartContainer Implementation\n\n**File:** `internal/cri/server/container_start.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) StartContainer(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.StartContainerRequest)\n    (*runtime.StartContainerResponse, error) {\n\n    containerID := r.ContainerId\n\n    // 1. Lookup container\n    container, err := c.containerStore.Get(containerID)\n\n    // 2. Create and start task\n    task, err := container.New(ctx, runtime.TaskServiceClient)\n\n    // 3. Start the task\n    err = task.Start(ctx)\n\n    // 4. Update container state\n    container.State = CONTAINER_RUNNING\n    c.containerStore.Update(containerID, container)\n\n    // 5. Return response\n    return &runtime.StartContainerResponse{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n### 3.4 Instrumentation Layer\n\n**File:** `internal/cri/instrument/instrumented_service.go`\n\nThe instrumented service wraps the core service to add metrics and tracing:\n\n```go\ntype instrumentedService struct {\n    runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer\n    runtime.UnimplementedImageServiceServer\n    service GRPCServices\n}\n\n// Each RPC method is wrapped:\nfunc (s *instrumentedService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest)\n    (*runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // Add tracing\n    // Add metrics\n    // Call underlying service\n\n    return s.service.RunPodSandbox(ctx, r)\n}\n```\n\n### 3.5 gRPC Server Registration\n\n**File:** `plugins/cri/cri.go` (continued)\n\n```go\ntype criGRPCServer struct {\n    runtime.RuntimeServiceServer\n    runtime.ImageServiceServer\n    io.Closer\n    initializer\n}\n\nfunc (c *criGRPCServer) register(s *grpc.Server) error {\n    // Wrap service with instrumentation\n    instrumented := instrument.NewService(c)\n\n    // Register on gRPC server\n    runtime.RegisterRuntimeServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    runtime.RegisterImageServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n\n    return nil\n}\n\nfunc (c *criGRPCServer) Register(s *grpc.Server) error {\n    return c.register(s)\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Part 4: Vendoring of CRI API Types in Kubernetes\n\n### Vendoring Mechanism\n\nKubernetes vendors the CRI API types to ensure consistency and allow kubelet to use them directly without external dependencies.\n\n**Vendoring Path:** `vendor/k8s.io/cri-api/`\n\nHowever, in this specific kubernetes repo, the CRI API is in the staging area at:\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/\n```\n\nThis is published as a separate package (`k8s.io/cri-api`) and then vendored by other projects.\n\n### Key Vendored Types\n\nThe following types are vendored from `k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1`:\n\n1. **Pod Sandbox Types**\n   - `PodSandboxConfig` - Pod sandbox configuration\n   - `PodSandbox` - Pod sandbox state\n   - `PodSandboxStatus` - Pod sandbox status\n   - `PodSandboxStateValue` - Running/NotReady states\n   - `PodSandboxMetadata` - Pod metadata (UID, namespace, name, attempt)\n\n2. **Container Types**\n   - `ContainerConfig` - Container configuration\n   - `Container` - Container state\n   - `ContainerStatus` - Container status and state\n   - `ContainerStateValue` - Created/Running/Exited states\n   - `ContainerMetadata` - Container metadata\n\n3. **Image Types**\n   - `ImageSpec` - Image reference and auth\n   - `Image` - Image information\n   - `ImageFilter` - Filter for listing images\n   - `AuthConfig` - Image pull credentials\n\n4. **Network Types**\n   - `NetworkConfig` - Network configuration\n   - `IPAddress` - Pod IP address\n   - `Int64Value` - Wrapper for optional int64\n\n5. **Resource Types**\n   - `LinuxContainerResources` - CPU/Memory limits\n   - `WindowsContainerResources` - Windows-specific resources\n   - `ContainerResources` - Platform-independent resources\n\n6. **Runtime Types**\n   - `VersionResponse` - Runtime version info\n   - `StatusResponse` - Runtime status\n   - `RuntimeConfig` - Runtime configuration\n   - `RuntimeConfigResponse` - Runtime configuration details\n   - `RuntimeHandler` - Available runtime handlers\n\n### How Kubernetes Uses Vendored Types\n\nIn containerd's CRI plugin:\n```go\nimport runtime \"k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1\"\n\n// containerd receives CRI requests with these vendored types\nfunc (c *criService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n    r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // r contains runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest from kubernetes\n    // response uses runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse\n}\n```\n\nThe vendored types in containerd are actually the exact same types as in the Kubernetes CRI API package, ensuring wire-format compatibility.\n\n---\n\n## Part 5: Complete Interface Contract\n\n### Interface Hierarchy\n\n```\ngRPC Wire Protocol (api.proto)\n    ↓\nGenerated Go Server Interface (RuntimeServiceServer in api_grpc.pb.go)\n    ↓\nProtocol Buffer Messages (types in api.pb.go)\n    ↓\nKubernetes Go Interfaces (RuntimeService, ContainerManager, etc. in services.go)\n    ↓\ncontainerd Implementation (criService in internal/cri/server/service.go)\n```\n\n### Method Mapping Example: RunPodSandbox\n\n**gRPC Definition (api.proto):**\n```protobuf\nrpc RunPodSandbox(RunPodSandboxRequest) returns (RunPodSandboxResponse) {}\n```\n\n**Generated Server Interface (api_grpc.pb.go):**\n```go\ntype RuntimeServiceServer interface {\n    RunPodSandbox(context.Context, *RunPodSandboxRequest) (*RunPodSandboxResponse, error)\n}\n```\n\n**Kubernetes Go Interface (services.go):**\n```go\ntype PodSandboxManager interface {\n    RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, config *runtimeapi.PodSandboxConfig,\n        runtimeHandler string) (string, error)\n}\n```\n\n**containerd Implementation (sandbox_run.go):**\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n    r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // Implementation that:\n    // 1. Generates sandbox ID\n    // 2. Sets up network via CNI\n    // 3. Creates containerd container/task\n    // 4. Stores metadata\n    // 5. Returns sandbox ID\n}\n```\n\n**kubelet Usage (pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/):**\n```go\npodSandboxID, err := c.runtimeService.RunPodSandbox(ctx,\n    &runtimeapi.PodSandboxConfig{...},\n    runtimeHandler)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Part 6: Data Flow Example: Creating and Running a Pod\n\n### Complete Request/Response Flow\n\n```\n1. KUBELET INITIATES POD CREATION\n   └─ pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_manager.go\n      └─ runtimeService.RunPodSandbox(ctx, config, handler)\n\n2. gRPC CLIENT SEND\n   └─ staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go\n      └─ Calls remoteRuntimeService.RunPodSandbox()\n         └─ Marshals request to protobuf\n         └─ Sends gRPC call to containerd socket\n\n3. gRPC SERVER RECEIVE (containerd)\n   └─ plugins/cri/cri.go: criGRPCServer\n      └─ instrument/instrumented_service.go: instrumentedService (wraps)\n         └─ internal/cri/server/service.go: criService.RunPodSandbox() (implementation)\n\n4. CONTAINERD PROCESSING\n   └─ Receives: runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest\n      ├─ Extract config\n      ├─ Generate sandbox ID\n      ├─ Reserve name\n      ├─ Setup CNI network\n      ├─ Create containerd container\n      ├─ Start task\n      └─ Store in sandboxStore\n\n5. gRPC RESPONSE SEND\n   └─ Return: runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse{PodSandboxId: id}\n      └─ Marshal to protobuf\n      └─ Send over gRPC\n\n6. KUBELET RECEIVE\n   └─ Unmarshals response\n   └─ Stores sandbox ID for future container operations\n   └─ Proceeds with container creation\n```\n\n---\n\n## Part 7: Key Design Patterns\n\n### 1. Idempotency\n- **StopPodSandbox**, **RemovePodSandbox**: Safe to call multiple times\n- Returns success even if already in desired state\n- Implements cleanup-first approach\n\n### 2. Resource Tracking\n- Sandbox and container stores track all resources\n- Name index prevents duplicate names\n- Lease service ensures proper cleanup on failure\n\n### 3. Graceful Shutdown\n- Tasks receive SIGTERM with configurable timeout\n- Force SIGKILL after grace period\n- Ensures clean container termination\n\n### 4. Network Integration\n- CNI plugins handle network setup/teardown\n- Dual network (plugin + IP allocation)\n- Per-runtime network plugin configuration\n\n### 5. Instrumentation Layer\n- Wraps actual implementation\n- Adds metrics and tracing without modifying core logic\n- Maintains separation of concerns\n\n### 6. Modular Implementation\n- Each RPC method in separate file (e.g., sandbox_run.go, container_create.go)\n- Platform-specific implementations (_linux.go, _windows.go, _other.go)\n- Cleanly separates concerns\n\n---\n\n## Part 8: Summary\n\n### The CRI as a Contract\n\nThe Kubernetes CRI provides a **contract** between kubelet and container runtimes:\n\n1. **gRPC Protocol** - Defines wire format and network communication\n2. **Message Types** - Specifies exact data structures exchanged\n3. **RPC Methods** - Enumerates operations runtimes must support\n4. **Semantic Guarantees** - Documents behavior expectations (e.g., idempotency)\n\n### containerd's Role\n\ncontainerd implements this contract:\n\n1. **Registers as CRI Plugin** - Exposes itself via containerd plugin system\n2. **Implements Interface** - Satisfies `RuntimeServiceServer` interface\n3. **Manages Resources** - Creates/starts/stops containers and sandboxes\n4. **Integrates Systems** - Combines CNI, OCI, snapshots, and tasks\n5. **Provides Instrumentation** - Metrics, tracing, and logging\n\n### Kubernetes Integration\n\nKubernetes uses the CRI to:\n\n1. **Abstract Container Runtime** - No direct Docker/runc dependency\n2. **Manage Pod Lifecycle** - Create, run, and delete pods\n3. **Support Multiple Runtimes** - CRI allows swappable implementations\n4. **Maintain Consistency** - All runtimes implement same interface\n\n### Architecture Benefits\n\n- **Decoupling** - Kubernetes doesn't depend on specific runtime\n- **Extensibility** - New runtimes can implement CRI\n- **Testing** - Easy to mock/fake implementations\n- **Stability** - Defined contracts prevent breaking changes\n- **Evolution** - gRPC allows safe API additions\n\n---\n\n## Part 9: Key Files Reference\n\n### Kubernetes Repository\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto` - gRPC definitions\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api_grpc.pb.go` - Generated Go server interface\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.pb.go` - Generated protobuf messages\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/services.go` - High-level Go interfaces\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go` - kubelet's CRI client\n\n### containerd Repository\n- `plugins/cri/cri.go` - Plugin registration and gRPC server setup\n- `internal/cri/server/service.go` - Core CRI service implementation\n- `internal/cri/server/sandbox_*.go` - Sandbox-related operations (19 files)\n- `internal/cri/server/container_*.go` - Container-related operations (20+ files)\n- `internal/cri/instrument/instrumented_service.go` - Metrics and tracing wrapper\n- `vendor/k8s.io/cri-api/` - Vendored Kubernetes CRI API types\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThe Kubernetes CRI represents a well-designed distributed system contract that:\n\n1. **Clearly Defines Requirements** - gRPC + protobuf provides precise specification\n2. **Enables Multiple Implementations** - Different runtimes can satisfy same interface\n3. **Maintains Compatibility** - Versioned API prevents breaking changes\n4. **Supports Evolution** - Streaming and stats methods added over time\n5. **Facilitates Testing** - Interfaces enable mocking and testing\n\ncontainerd's implementation demonstrates how a complex system (container lifecycle management, networking, resource control) can cleanly implement the CRI contract while maintaining internal flexibility and extensibility.\n\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3457,"cache_read_input_tokens":69583,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3457},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"72366629-4769-4ce6-93ed-c37c9afe3f27","uuid":"ba8571cd-5cdf-4250-a87a-c886112e0072"}

┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │\n│ │ criGRPCServer (runtime.RuntimeServiceServer impl)   │ │\n│ └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ wrapper)     │\n        └─────────────┬──────────────┘\n                      │\n        ┌─────────────▼──────────────────┐\n        │ criService struct              │\n        │ (main implementation)       ▼\nSandbox Ops      Container Ops    Image/Stats Ops\n```\n\n### 3.1 Plugin Registration & Initialization\n\n**File:** `plugins/cri/cri.go`\n\n```go\n// Registration entry point\nfunc init() {\n    defaultConfig := criconfig.DefaultServerConfig()\n    registry.Register(&plugin.Registration{\n        Type: plugins.GRPCPlugin,\n        ID:   \"cri\",\n        Requires: []plugin.Type{\n            plugins.CRIServicePlugin,       // Runtime service\n            plugins.PodSandboxPlugin,       // Pod sandbox support\n            plugins.SandboxControllerPlugin, // Sandbox controllers\n            plugins.NRIApiPlugin,           // Node Resource Interface\n            plugins.EventPlugin,            // Event handling\n            plugins.ServicePlugin,          // Services\n            plugins.LeasePlugin,            // Lease management\n            plugins.SandboxStorePlugin,     // Sandbox storage\n            plugins.TransferPlugin,         // Content transfer\n            plugins.WarningPlugin,          // Warning service\n        },\n        ConfigMigration: configMigration,\n        InitFn:          initCRIService,\n    })\n}\n\n// Initialization function\nfunc initCRIService(ic *plugin.InitContext) (interface{}, error) {\n    // 1. Load runtime service plugin\n    criRuntimePlugin, err := ic.GetByID(plugins.CRIServicePlugin, \"runtime\")\n\n    // 2. Load image service plugin\n    criImagePlugin, err := ic.GetByID(plugins.CRIServicePlugin, \"images\")\n\n    // 3. Create containerd client\n    client, err := containerd.New(\"\",\n        containerd.WithDefaultNamespace(constants.K8sContainerdNamespace),\n        containerd.WithDefaultPlatform(platforms.Default()),\n        containerd.WithInMemoryServices(ic),\n    )\n\n    // 4. Get sandbox controllers\n    sbControllers, err := getSandboxControllers(ic)\n\n    // 5. Create CRI service\n    s, rs, err := server.NewCRIService(&server.CRIServiceOptions{\n        RuntimeService:     criRuntimePlugin.(server.RuntimeService),\n        ImageService:       criImagePlugin.(server.ImageService),\n        StreamingConfig:    streamingConfig,\n        NRI:                getNRIAPI(ic),\n        Client:             client,\n        SandboxControllers: sbControllers,\n    })\n\n    // 6. Wrap in gRPC server\n    service := &criGRPCServer{\n        RuntimeServiceServer: rs,\n        ImageServiceServer:   is,\n        Closer:               s,\n        initializer:          s,\n    }\n\n    return service, nil\n}\n```\n\n### 3.2 Core CRI Service Implementation\n\n**File:** `internal/cri/server/service.go`\n\nThe `criService` struct implements the core logic:\n\n```go\ntype criService struct {\n    // Embedded unimplemented server to satisfy gRPC requirements\n    runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer\n    runtime.UnimplementedImageServiceServer\n\n    // Service dependencies\n    RuntimeService\n    ImageService\n\n    // Configuration\n    config criconfig.Config\n    imageFSPaths map[string]string\n    os osinterface.OS\n\n    // Storage and indexing\n    sandboxStore *sandboxstore.Store\n    sandboxNameIndex *registrar.Registrar  // Ensures unique sandbox names\n    containerStore *containerstore.Store\n    containerNameIndex *registrar.Registrar // Ensures unique container names\n\n    // Network management\n    netPlugin map[string]cni.CNI\n\n    // containerd client\n    client *containerd.Client\n\n    // Streaming support\n    streamServer streaming.Server\n\n    // Event monitoring\n    eventMonitor *events.EventMonitor\n\n    // Initialization flag\n    initialized atomic.Bool\n\n    // Network config monitoring\n    cniNetConfMonitor map[string]*cniNetConfSyncer\n\n    // Capabilities\n    allCaps []string\n\n    // Container events queue\n    containerEventsQ eventq.EventQueue[*runtime.ContainerEventResponse]\n\n    // Node Resource Interface\n    nri *nri.API\n\n    // Sandbox service\n    sandboxService sandboxService\n\n    // Runtime handlers and features\n    runtimeHandlers map[string]*runtime.RuntimeHandler\n    runtimeFeatures *runtime.RuntimeFeatures\n\n    // Stats collection\n    statsCollector *StatsCollector\n}\n```\n\n**Constructor:** `NewCRIService(options *CRIServiceOptions)`\n\nCreates a fully initialized CRI service with:\n- Sandbox and container stores\n- CNI network plugin initialization\n- Streaming server setup\n- Event monitoring\n- Stats collection\n\n### 3.3 RPC Method Implementation Examples\n\n#### RunPodSandbox Implementation\n\n**File:** `internal/cri/server/sandbox_run.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest)\n    (*runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    config := r.GetConfig()\n\n    // 1. Generate unique ID and name\n    id := util.GenerateID()\n    metadata := config.GetMetadata()\n    name := makeSandboxName(metadata)\n\n    // 2. Reserve the name (prevents concurrent creation with same name)\n    if err := c.sandboxNameIndex.Reserve(name, id); err != nil {\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to reserve sandbox name %q: %w\", name, err)\n    }\n    defer cleanup()\n\n    // 3. Create lease for sandbox lifecycle\n    leaseSvc := c.client.LeasesService()\n    ls, lerr := leaseSvc.Create(ctx, leases.WithID(id))\n\n    // 4. Setup network (CNI)\n    // - Call network plugin to setup network namespace\n    // - Allocate IP addresses for the pod\n\n    // 5. Create sandbox container (OCI spec from config)\n    // - Convert CRI PodSandboxConfig to OCI spec\n    // - Create containerd container\n\n    // 6. Start sandbox task\n    // - Start the sandbox task in containerd\n    // - Ensure sandbox is in ready state\n\n    // 7. Register sandbox in store\n    sandboxStore.Add(id, &Sandbox{\n        ID:     id,\n        Config: config,\n        State:  SANDBOX_READY,\n    })\n\n    // 8. Return response\n    return &runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse{\n        PodSandboxId: id,\n    }, nil\n}\n```\n\n**Key Details:**\n- Generates unique sandbox ID using `util.GenerateID()`\n- Reserves sandbox name to prevent concurrent duplicates\n- Creates lease for resource tracking\n- Sets up network using CNI plugins\n- Creates and starts sandbox task in containerd\n- Stores sandbox metadata in sandboxStore\n- Returns sandbox ID to caller (kubelet)\n\n#### StopPodSandbox Implementation\n\n**File:** `internal/cri/server/sandbox_stop.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) StopPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.StopPodSandboxRequest)\n    (*runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    podSandboxID := r.PodSandboxId\n    gracePeriod := r.Timeout\n\n    // 1. Lookup sandbox in store\n    sandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(podSandboxID)\n\n    // 2. Stop all containers in sandbox (forced termination)\n    for _, container := range c.containerStore.ListByPodID(podSandboxID) {\n        c.StopContainer(ctx, container.ID, gracePeriod)\n    }\n\n    // 3. Stop sandbox task in containerd\n    // - Send SIGTERM to sandbox\n    // - Wait for grace period\n    // - Force kill if still running\n\n    // 4. Teardown network (CNI)\n    // - Release IP addresses\n    // - Cleanup network namespace\n\n    // 5. Update sandbox state\n    sandbox.State = SANDBOX_NOTREADY\n    c.sandboxStore.Update(podSandboxID, sandbox)\n\n    // 6. Idempotent: return nil even if already stopped\n    return &runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n**Key Details:**\n- Idempotent operation (safe to call multiple times)\n- Forcibly terminates all containers in sandbox\n- Gracefully stops sandbox with timeout\n- Tears down network resources (CNI cleanup)\n- Updates sandbox state without removing from store\n\n#### RemovePodSandbox Implementation\n\n**File:** `internal/cri/server/sandbox_remove.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RemovePodSandbox(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.RemovePodSandboxRequest)\n    (*runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    podSandboxID := r.PodSandboxId\n\n    // 1. Lookup sandbox\n    sandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(podSandboxID)\n\n    // 2. Must be stopped first\n    if sandbox.State != SANDBOX_NOTREADY {\n        return nil, fmt.Errorf(\"sandbox %q is still running\", podSandboxID)\n    }\n\n    // 3. Delete all containers in sandbox\n    for _, container := range c.containerStore.ListByPodID(podSandboxID) {\n        c.RemoveContainer(ctx, container.ID)\n    }\n\n    // 4. Delete sandbox container from containerd\n    // - Delete container task\n    // - Delete container\n    // - Delete snapshots\n\n    // 5. Release lease\n    leaseSvc := c.client.LeasesService()\n    leaseSvc.Delete(ctx, leases.WithID(podSandboxID))\n\n    // 6. Release sandbox name\n    c.sandboxNameIndex.ReleaseByName(sandbox.Name)\n\n    // 7. Remove from store\n    c.sandboxStore.Delete(podSandboxID)\n\n    // 8. Idempotent: return nil even if already removed\n    return &runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n**Key Details:**\n- Deletes all containers before removing sandbox\n- Removes containerd resources (snapshots, leases)\n- Releases reserved sandbox name\n- Idempotent (safe to call on already-removed sandbox)\n\n#### CreateContainer Implementation\n\n**File:** `internal/cri/server/container_create.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) CreateContainer(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.CreateContainerRequest)\n    (*runtime.CreateContainerResponse, error) {\n\n    podSandboxID := r.PodSandboxId\n    config := r.Config\n    sandboxConfig := r.SandboxConfig\n\n    // 1. Lookup parent sandbox\n    sandbox, err := c.sandboxStore.Get(podSandboxID)\n\n    // 2. Generate container ID and name\n    containerID := util.GenerateID()\n    containerName := makeContainerName(metadata, sandbox.Config)\n\n    // 3. Reserve container name\n    if err := c.containerNameIndex.Reserve(containerName, containerID); err != nil {\n        return nil, err\n    }\n\n    // 4. Build OCI spec from CRI ContainerConfig\n    // - Start with runtime's base spec\n    // - Apply image config\n    // - Apply container config (env, mounts, resources, etc.)\n    // - Setup hostname, DNS, security context\n\n    // 5. Create container image snapshot\n    // - Pull image if needed\n    // - Create diff snapshot for container layers\n\n    // 6. Create containerd container\n    container, err := c.client.Containers().Create(ctx, &containers.Container{\n        ID:     containerID,\n        Image:  config.Image.Image,\n        Spec:   &ociSpec,\n        Snapshotter: snapshotterName,\n    })\n\n    // 7. Store container metadata\n    c.containerStore.Add(containerID, &Container{\n        ID:            containerID,\n        PodSandboxID:  podSandboxID,\n        Config:        config,\n        SandboxConfig: sandboxConfig,\n        ImageRef:      imageID,\n        State:         CONTAINER_CREATED,\n    })\n\n    // 8. Return container ID\n    return &runtime.CreateContainerResponse{\n        ContainerId: containerID,\n    }, nil\n}\n```\n\n**Key Details:**\n- Container created but NOT started yet\n- Generates OCI spec from CRI config\n- Pulls image if not available\n- Creates snapshots for container layers\n- Stores metadata for later retrieval\n- Actual task execution happens in StartContainer\n\n#### StartContainer Implementation\n\n**File:** `internal/cri/server/container_start.go`\n\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) StartContainer(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.StartContainerRequest)\n    (*runtime.StartContainerResponse, error) {\n\n    containerID := r.ContainerId\n\n    // 1. Lookup container\n    container, err := c.containerStore.Get(containerID)\n\n    // 2. Create and start task\n    task, err := container.New(ctx, runtime.TaskServiceClient)\n\n    // 3. Start the task\n    err = task.Start(ctx)\n\n    // 4. Update container state\n    container.State = CONTAINER_RUNNING\n    c.containerStore.Update(containerID, container)\n\n    // 5. Return response\n    return &runtime.StartContainerResponse{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n### 3.4 Instrumentation Layer\n\n**File:** `internal/cri/instrument/instrumented_service.go`\n\nThe instrumented service wraps the core service to add metrics and tracing:\n\n```go\ntype instrumentedService struct {\n    runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer\n    runtime.UnimplementedImageServiceServer\n    service GRPCServices\n}\n\n// Each RPC method is wrapped:\nfunc (s *instrumentedService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest)\n    (*runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // Add tracing\n    // Add metrics\n    // Call underlying service\n\n    return s.service.RunPodSandbox(ctx, r)\n}\n```\n\n### 3.5 gRPC Server Registration\n\n**File:** `plugins/cri/cri.go` (continued)\n\n```go\ntype criGRPCServer struct {\n    runtime.RuntimeServiceServer\n    runtime.ImageServiceServer\n    io.Closer\n    initializer\n}\n\nfunc (c *criGRPCServer) register(s *grpc.Server) error {\n    // Wrap service with instrumentation\n    instrumented := instrument.NewService(c)\n\n    // Register on gRPC server\n    runtime.RegisterRuntimeServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n    runtime.RegisterImageServiceServer(s, instrumented)\n\n    return nil\n}\n\nfunc (c *criGRPCServer) Register(s *grpc.Server) error {\n    return c.register(s)\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Part 4: Vendoring of CRI API Types in Kubernetes\n\n### Vendoring Mechanism\n\nKubernetes vendors the CRI API types to ensure consistency and allow kubelet to use them directly without external dependencies.\n\n**Vendoring Path:** `vendor/k8s.io/cri-api/`\n\nHowever, in this specific kubernetes repo, the CRI API is in the staging area at:\n```\nstaging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/\n```\n\nThis is published as a separate package (`k8s.io/cri-api`) and then vendored by other projects.\n\n### Key Vendored Types\n\nThe following types are vendored from `k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1`:\n\n1. **Pod Sandbox Types**\n   - `PodSandboxConfig` - Pod sandbox configuration\n   - `PodSandbox` - Pod sandbox state\n   - `PodSandboxStatus` - Pod sandbox status\n   - `PodSandboxStateValue` - Running/NotReady states\n   - `PodSandboxMetadata` - Pod metadata (UID, namespace, name, attempt)\n\n2. **Container Types**\n   - `ContainerConfig` - Container configuration\n   - `Container` - Container state\n   - `ContainerStatus` - Container status and state\n   - `ContainerStateValue` - Created/Running/Exited states\n   - `ContainerMetadata` - Container metadata\n\n3. **Image Types**\n   - `ImageSpec` - Image reference and auth\n   - `Image` - Image information\n   - `ImageFilter` - Filter for listing images\n   - `AuthConfig` - Image pull credentials\n\n4. **Network Types**\n   - `NetworkConfig` - Network configuration\n   - `IPAddress` - Pod IP address\n   - `Int64Value` - Wrapper for optional int64\n\n5. **Resource Types**\n   - `LinuxContainerResources` - CPU/Memory limits\n   - `WindowsContainerResources` - Windows-specific resources\n   - `ContainerResources` - Platform-independent resources\n\n6. **Runtime Types**\n   - `VersionResponse` - Runtime version info\n   - `StatusResponse` - Runtime status\n   - `RuntimeConfig` - Runtime configuration\n   - `RuntimeConfigResponse` - Runtime configuration details\n   - `RuntimeHandler` - Available runtime handlers\n\n### How Kubernetes Uses Vendored Types\n\nIn containerd's CRI plugin:\n```go\nimport runtime \"k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1\"\n\n// containerd receives CRI requests with these vendored types\nfunc (c *criService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n    r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // r contains runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest from kubernetes\n    // response uses runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse\n}\n```\n\nThe vendored types in containerd are actually the exact same types as in the Kubernetes CRI API package, ensuring wire-format compatibility.\n\n---\n\n## Part 5: Complete Interface Contract\n\n### Interface Hierarchy\n\n```\ngRPC Wire Protocol (api.proto)\n    ↓\nGenerated Go Server Interface (RuntimeServiceServer in api_grpc.pb.go)\n    ↓\nProtocol Buffer Messages (types in api.pb.go)\n    ↓\nKubernetes Go Interfaces (RuntimeService, ContainerManager, etc. in services.go)\n    ↓\ncontainerd Implementation (criService in internal/cri/server/service.go)\n```\n\n### Method Mapping Example: RunPodSandbox\n\n**gRPC Definition (api.proto):**\n```protobuf\nrpc RunPodSandbox(RunPodSandboxRequest) returns (RunPodSandboxResponse) {}\n```\n\n**Generated Server Interface (api_grpc.pb.go):**\n```go\ntype RuntimeServiceServer interface {\n    RunPodSandbox(context.Context, *RunPodSandboxRequest) (*RunPodSandboxResponse, error)\n}\n```\n\n**Kubernetes Go Interface (services.go):**\n```go\ntype PodSandboxManager interface {\n    RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, config *runtimeapi.PodSandboxConfig,\n        runtimeHandler string) (string, error)\n}\n```\n\n**containerd Implementation (sandbox_run.go):**\n```go\nfunc (c *criService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context,\n    r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n\n    // Implementation that:\n    // 1. Generates sandbox ID\n    // 2. Sets up network via CNI\n    // 3. Creates containerd container/task\n    // 4. Stores metadata\n    // 5. Returns sandbox ID\n}\n```\n\n**kubelet Usage (pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/):**\n```go\npodSandboxID, err := c.runtimeService.RunPodSandbox(ctx,\n    &runtimeapi.PodSandboxConfig{...},\n    runtimeHandler)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Part 6: Data Flow Example: Creating and Running a Pod\n\n### Complete Request/Response Flow\n\n```\n1. KUBELET INITIATES POD CREATION\n   └─ pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_manager.go\n      └─ runtimeService.RunPodSandbox(ctx, config, handler)\n\n2. gRPC CLIENT SEND\n   └─ staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go\n      └─ Calls remoteRuntimeService.RunPodSandbox()\n         └─ Marshals request to protobuf\n         └─ Sends gRPC call to containerd socket\n\n3. gRPC SERVER RECEIVE (containerd)\n   └─ plugins/cri/cri.go: criGRPCServer\n      └─ instrument/instrumented_service.go: instrumentedService (wraps)\n         └─ internal/cri/server/service.go: criService.RunPodSandbox() (implementation)\n\n4. CONTAINERD PROCESSING\n   └─ Receives: runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest\n      ├─ Extract config\n      ├─ Generate sandbox ID\n      ├─ Reserve name\n      ├─ Setup CNI network\n      ├─ Create containerd container\n      ├─ Start task\n      └─ Store in sandboxStore\n\n5. gRPC RESPONSE SEND\n   └─ Return: runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse{PodSandboxId: id}\n      └─ Marshal to protobuf\n      └─ Send over gRPC\n\n6. KUBELET RECEIVE\n   └─ Unmarshals response\n   └─ Stores sandbox ID for future container operations\n   └─ Proceeds with container creation\n```\n\n---\n\n## Part 7: Key Design Patterns\n\n### 1. Idempotency\n- **StopPodSandbox**, **RemovePodSandbox**: Safe to call multiple times\n- Returns success even if already in desired state\n- Implements cleanup-first approach\n\n### 2. Resource Tracking\n- Sandbox and container stores track all resources\n- Name index prevents duplicate names\n- Lease service ensures proper cleanup on failure\n\n### 3. Graceful Shutdown\n- Tasks receive SIGTERM with configurable timeout\n- Force SIGKILL after grace period\n- Ensures clean container termination\n\n### 4. Network Integration\n- CNI plugins handle network setup/teardown\n- Dual network (plugin + IP allocation)\n- Per-runtime network plugin configuration\n\n### 5. Instrumentation Layer\n- Wraps actual implementation\n- Adds metrics and tracing without modifying core logic\n- Maintains separation of concerns\n\n### 6. Modular Implementation\n- Each RPC method in separate file (e.g., sandbox_run.go, container_create.go)\n- Platform-specific implementations (_linux.go, _windows.go, _other.go)\n- Cleanly separates concerns\n\n---\n\n## Part 8: Summary\n\n### The CRI as a Contract\n\nThe Kubernetes CRI provides a **contract** between kubelet and container runtimes:\n\n1. **gRPC Protocol** - Defines wire format and network communication\n2. **Message Types** - Specifies exact data structures exchanged\n3. **RPC Methods** - Enumerates operations runtimes must support\n4. **Semantic Guarantees** - Documents behavior expectations (e.g., idempotency)\n\n### containerd's Role\n\ncontainerd implements this contract:\n\n1. **Registers as CRI Plugin** - Exposes itself via containerd plugin system\n2. **Implements Interface** - Satisfies `RuntimeServiceServer` interface\n3. **Manages Resources** - Creates/starts/stops containers and sandboxes\n4. **Integrates Systems** - Combines CNI, OCI, snapshots, and tasks\n5. **Provides Instrumentation** - Metrics, tracing, and logging\n\n### Kubernetes Integration\n\nKubernetes uses the CRI to:\n\n1. **Abstract Container Runtime** - No direct Docker/runc dependency\n2. **Manage Pod Lifecycle** - Create, run, and delete pods\n3. **Support Multiple Runtimes** - CRI allows swappable implementations\n4. **Maintain Consistency** - All runtimes implement same interface\n\n### Architecture Benefits\n\n- **Decoupling** - Kubernetes doesn't depend on specific runtime\n- **Extensibility** - New runtimes can implement CRI\n- **Testing** - Easy to mock/fake implementations\n- **Stability** - Defined contracts prevent breaking changes\n- **Evolution** - gRPC allows safe API additions\n\n---\n\n## Part 9: Key Files Reference\n\n### Kubernetes Repository\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto` - gRPC definitions\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api_grpc.pb.go` - Generated Go server interface\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.pb.go` - Generated protobuf messages\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/services.go` - High-level Go interfaces\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_runtime.go` - kubelet's CRI client\n\n### containerd Repository\n- `plugins/cri/cri.go` - Plugin registration and gRPC server setup\n- `internal/cri/server/service.go` - Core CRI service implementation\n- `internal/cri/server/sandbox_*.go` - Sandbox-related operations (19 files)\n- `internal/cri/server/container_*.go` - Container-related operations (20+ files)\n- `internal/cri/instrument/instrumented_service.go` - Metrics and tracing wrapper\n- `vendor/k8s.io/cri-api/` - Vendored Kubernetes CRI API types\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThe Kubernetes CRI represents a well-designed distributed system contract that:\n\n1. **Clearly Defines Requirements** - gRPC + protobuf provides precise specification\n2. **Enables Multiple Implementations** - Different runtimes can satisfy same interface\n3. **Maintains Compatibility** - Versioned API prevents breaking changes\n4. **Supports Evolution** - Streaming and stats methods added over time\n5. **Facilitates Testing** - Interfaces enable mocking and testing\n\ncontainerd's implementation demonstrates how a complex system (container lifecycle management, networking, resource control) can cleanly implement the CRI contract while maintaining internal flexibility and extensibility.\n\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
